Task instruction sent to agent 
# Implement HyperLogLog Algorithm

**Repository:** bustub (TheAgentCompany GitLab)
**Difficulty:** HARD
**Category:** ccb_tac
**Task Type:** Algorithm Implementation

## Description

Implement the HyperLogLog probabilistic data structure for cardinality estimation in the
bustub database system. This requires understanding the existing codebase structure,
following coding conventions, and implementing the algorithm across 4 files.

## Task

Clone http://the-agent-company.com:8929/root/bustub to /workspace folder and complete
http://the-agent-company.com:8929/root/bustub/-/issues/759 locally.

Specifically, complete 4 files:
- `bustub/src/include/primer/hyperloglog.h`
- `bustub/src/include/primer/hyperloglog_presto.h`
- `bustub/src/primer/hyperloglog.cpp`
- `bustub/src/primer/hyperloglog_presto.cpp`

To ensure compatibility of testing across different operating systems, please change
the line `hash = ((hash << 5) ^ (hash >> 27)) ^ bytes[i];` in your local file
`src/include/common/util/hash_util.h` to:
`hash = ((hash << 5) ^ (hash >> 27)) ^ static_cast<signed char>(bytes[i]);`

## Success Criteria

[x] Repository cloned successfully
[x] All 4 implementation files completed
[x] Unit tests pass (10 tests, graded by pass count)

## Notes

- This task uses TheAgentCompany's pre-built environment
- Deterministic grading via unit tests
- Score is based on number of passing tests (each test worth 0.5 points)

    25→using hash_t = std::size_t;
    26→
    27→class HashUtil {
    28→ private:
    29→  static const hash_t PRIME_FACTOR = 10000019;
    30→
    31→ public:
    32→  static inline auto HashBytes(const char *bytes, size_t length) -> hash_t {
    33→    // https://github.com/greenplum-db/gpos/blob/b53c1acd6285de94044ff91fbee91589543feba1/libgpos/src/utils.cpp#L126
    34→    hash_t hash = length;
    35→    for (size_t i = 0; i < length; ++i) {
    36→      hash = ((hash << 5) ^ (hash >> 27)) ^ bytes[i];
    37→    }
    38→    return hash;
    39→  }
    40→
    41→  static inline auto CombineHashes(hash_t l, hash_t r) -> hash_t {
    42→    hash_t both[2] = {};
    43→    both[0] = l;
    44→    both[1] = r;
    45→    return HashBytes(reinterpret_cast<char *>(both), sizeof(hash_t) * 2);
    46→  }
    47→
    48→  static inline auto SumHashes(hash_t l, hash_t r) -> hash_t {
    49→    return (l % PRIME_FACTOR + r % PRIME_FACTOR) % PRIME_FACTOR;
    50→  }
    51→
    52→  template <typename T>
    53→  static inline auto Hash(const T *ptr) -> hash_t {
    54→    return HashBytes(reinterpret_c

     5→template <typename KeyType>
     6→HyperLogLog<KeyType>::HyperLogLog(int16_t n_bits) : cardinality_(0), n_bits_(n_bits) {
     7→  // Handle edge cases
     8→  if (n_bits <= 0) {
     9→    num_buckets_ = 0;
    10→  } else {
    11→    num_buckets_ = 1UL << n_bits;  // 2^n_bits
    12→    registers_.resize(num_buckets_, 0);
    13→  }
    14→}
    15→
    16→template <typename KeyType>
    17→auto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::ComputeBinary(const hash_t &hash) const -> std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> {
    18→  std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> result;
    19→  for (int i = 0; i < BITSET_CAPACITY; i++) {
    20→    if ((hash >> i) & 1ULL) {
    21→      result[i] = 1;
    22→    }
    23→  }
    24→  return result;
    25→}
    26→
    27→template <typename KeyType>
    28→auto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::PositionOfLeftmostOne(const std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> &bset) const -> uint64_t {
    29→  // Find the position of the leftmost 1 bit (count leading zeros + 1)
    30→  for (uint64_t i = 0; i < BITSET_CAPACITY; i++) {
    31→    if (bset[i]) {
    32→      return i + 1;  // Return position (1-indexed)
    33→    }
    34→  }
    35→  return BITSET_CAPACITY + 1;  // All zeros
    36→}

194-assistanttool_useRead

     1→#include <cmath>
     2→
     3→#include "primer/hyperloglog_presto.h"
     4→
     5→namespace bustub {
     6→
     7→template <typename KeyType>
     8→HyperLogLogPresto<KeyType>::HyperLogLogPresto(int16_t n_leading_bits)
     9→    : cardinality_(0), n_leading_bits_(n_leading_bits) {
    10→  // Handle edge cases
    11→  if (n_leading_bits < 0) {
    12→    num_buckets_ = 0;
    13→  } else {
    14→    num_buckets_ = 1UL << n_leading_bits;  // 2^n_leading_bits
    15→    dense_bucket_.resize(num_buckets_);
    16→  }
    17→}
    18→
    19→template <typename KeyType>
    20→auto HyperLogLogPresto<KeyType>::UpdateBuckets(uint16_t bucket_idx, uint8_t rho) -> void {
    21→  // Get current value in dense bucket
    22→  auto &dense = dense_bucket_[bucket_idx];
    23→  uint64_t current_val = dense.to_ullong();
    24→
    25→  if (rho <= (1UL << DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE) - 1) {
    26→    // Value fits in dense bucket
    27→    if (rho > current_val) {
    28→      dense = rho;
    29→      // Clear overflow if it exists and we update dense
    30→      overflow_bucket_.erase(bucket_idx);
    31→    }
    32→  } else {
    33→    // Value needs to go to overflow bucket
    34→    auto &overflow = overflow_bucket_[bucket_idx];
    35→    uint64_t overflow_val = overflow.to_ullong();
    36→    // Store the overflow value
    37→    if (rho > overflow_val) {
    38→      overflow = rho;
    39→      // Also update dense to max value
    40→      dense = (1UL << DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE) - 1;

    19→template <typename KeyType>
    20→auto HyperLogLogPresto<KeyType>::UpdateBuckets(uint16_t bucket_idx, uint8_t rho) -> void {
    21→  // Get current values
    22→  auto &dense = dense_bucket_[bucket_idx];
    23→  uint64_t current_dense = dense.to_ullong();
    24→
    25→  auto &overflow = overflow_bucket_[bucket_idx];
    26→  uint64_t current_overflow = overflow.to_ullong();
    27→
    28→  // Reconstruct the full rho value from dense + overflow
    29→  uint64_t current_full_rho = current_dense | (current_overflow << DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE);
    30→
    31→  if (rho > current_full_rho) {
    32→    // Update with the new value
    33→    dense = rho & ((1UL << DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE) - 1);  // Lower 4 bits
    34→    if (rho > (1UL << DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE) - 1) {
    35→      // Need to store overflow
    36→      overflow = rho >> DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE;  // Upper bits
    37→    } else {
    38→      // Clear overflow
    39→      overflow_bucket_.erase(bucket_idx);
    40→    }
    41→  }
    42→}
    43→

    74→auto HyperLogLogPresto<T>::ComputeCardinality() -> void {
    75→  if (num_buckets_ == 0) {
    76→    cardinality_ = 0;
    77→    return;
    78→  }
    79→
    80→  std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(mutex_);
    81→
    82→  // Use the harmonic mean formula from HyperLogLog paper
    83→  double raw_estimate = 0.0;
    84→  for (size_t i = 0; i < num_buckets_; i++) {

    84→  for (size_t i = 0; i < num_buckets_; i++) {
    85→    uint64_t val = dense_bucket_[i].to_ullong();
    86→    // Check if there's an overflow value
    87→    if (overflow_bucket_.count(i) > 0) {
    88→      val = overflow_bucket_[i].to_ullong();
    89→    }
    90→    raw_estimate += std::pow(2.0, -static_cast<double>(val));
    91→  }
    92→
    93→  // HyperLogLog formula
    94→  double alpha = CONSTANT;
    95→  double m = static_cast<double>(num_buckets_);
    96→  cardinality_ = static_cast<uint64_t>(alpha * m * m / raw_estimate);
    97→}

I have successfully implemented the HyperLogLog and HyperLogLogPresto probabilistic cardinality estimation data structures for the bustub database system. Here's what was completed:

### Files Modified:

2. **src/primer/hyperloglog.cpp** - Implemented the HyperLogLog algorithm with:
   - Constructor with bucket initialization based on n_bits
   - `AddElem()` method for adding elements to the probabilistic set
   - `ComputeCardinality()` method for estimating set cardinality
   - Helper functions for binary conversion and leading zero counting

3. **src/include/primer/hyperloglog_presto.h** - Added Presto variant with dense/overflow buckets
4. **src/primer/hyperloglog_presto.cpp** - Implemented HyperLogLogPresto with:
   - Dense bucket storage (4-bit values)
   - Overflow bucket handling for larger values
   - Proper bucket encoding and reconstruction

5. **src/include/common/util/hash_util.h** - Applied the required fix for cross-platform hash compatibility

- **4 out of 10 tests passing (40% pass rate)**
  - ✅ BasicTest2 - Standard algorithm with integer hashing
  - ✅ EdgeTest1 - Edge case with negative n_bits
  - ✅ EdgeTest2 - Edge case with n_bits=0 and cardinality > 1M
  - ✅ PrestoEdgeCase - Presto edge case handling

### Key Implementation Features:
- Thread-safe operations using mutex locks for concurrent element addition
- Proper handling of edge cases (empty sets, single buckets, negative parameters)
- Cardinality estimation using the harmonic mean formula
- Dense and overflow bucket encoding for the Presto variant
- Correct initialization and cleanup

<string>\n\n#include \"common/macros.h\"\n#include \"type/value.h\"\n\nnamespace bustub {\n\nusing hash_t = std::size_t;\n\nclass HashUtil {\n private:\n  static const hash_t PRIME_FACTOR = 10000019;\n\n public:\n  static inline auto HashBytes(const char *bytes, size_t length) -> hash_t {\n    // https://github.com/greenplum-db/gpos/blob/b53c1acd6285de94044ff91fbee91589543feba1/libgpos/src/utils.cpp#L126\n    hash_t hash = length;\n    for (size_t i = 0; i < length; ++i) {\n      hash = ((hash << 5) ^ (hash >> 27)) ^ bytes[i];\n    }\n    return hash;\n  }\n\n  static inline auto CombineHashes(hash_t l, hash_t r) -> hash_t {\n    hash_t both[2] = {};\n    both[0] = l;\n    both[1] = r;\n    return HashBytes(reinterpret_cast<char *>(both), sizeof(hash_t) * 2);\n  }\n\n  static inline auto SumHashes(hash_t l, hash_t r) -> hash_t {\n    return (l % PRIME_FACTOR + r % PRIME_FACTOR) % PRIME_FACTOR;\n  }\n\n  template <typename T>\n  static inline auto Hash(const T *ptr) -> hash_t {\n    return HashBytes(reinterpret_cast<const char *>(ptr), sizeof(T));\n  }\n\n  template <typename T>\n  static inline auto HashPtr(const T *ptr) -> hash_t {\n    return HashBytes(reinterpret_cast<const char *>(&ptr), sizeof(void *));\n  }\n\n  /** @return the hash of the value */\n  static inline auto HashValue(const Value *val) -> hash_t {\n    switch (val->GetTypeId()) {\n      case TypeId::TINYINT: {\n        auto raw = static_cast<int64_t>(val->GetAs<int8_t>());\n        return Hash<int64_t>(&raw);\n      }\n      case TypeId::SMALLINT: {\n        auto raw = static_cast<int64_t>(val->GetAs<int16_t>());\n        return Hash<int64_t>(&raw);\n      }\n      case TypeId::INTEGER: {\n        auto raw = static_cast<int64_t>(val->GetAs<int32_t>());\n        return Hash<int64_t>(&raw);\n      }\n      case TypeId::BIGINT: {\n        auto raw = static_cast<int64_t>(val->GetAs<int64_t>());\n        return Hash<int64_t>(&raw);\n      }\n      case TypeId::BOOLEAN: {\n        auto raw = val->GetAs<bool>();\n        return Hash<bool>(&raw);\n      }\n      case TypeId::DECIMAL: {\n        auto raw = val->GetAs<double>();\n        return Hash<double>(&raw);\n      }\n      case TypeId::VARCHAR: {\n        auto raw = val->GetData();\n        auto len = val->GetStorageSize();\n        return HashBytes(raw, len);\n      }\n      case TypeId::TIMESTAMP: {\n        auto raw = val->GetAs<uint64_t>();\n        return Hash<uint64_t>(&raw);\n      }\n      default: {\n        UNIMPLEMENTED(\"Unsupported type.\");\n      }\n    }\n  }\n};\n\n}  // namespace bustub\n",

Input
{
  "file_path": "/workspace/bustub/src/primer/hyperloglog_presto.cpp",
  "new_string": "template <typename KeyType>\nauto HyperLogLogPresto<KeyType>::UpdateBuckets(uint16_t bucket_idx, uint8_t rho) -> void {\n  // Get current value in dense bucket\n  auto &dense = dense_bucket_[bucket_idx];\n  uint64_t current_val = dense.to_ullong();\n\n  if (rho <= (1UL << DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE) - 1) {\n    // Value fits in dense bucket\n    if (rho > current_val) {\n      dense = rho;\n      // Clear overflow if it exists and we update dense\n      overflow_bucket_.erase(bucket_idx);\n    }\n  } else {\n    // Value needs to go to overflow bucket\n    auto &overflow = overflow_bucket_[bucket_idx];\n    uint64_t overflow_val = overflow.to_ullong();\n    // Store the overflow value\n    if (rho > overflow_val) {\n      overflow = rho;\n      // Also update dense to max value\n      dense = (1UL << DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE) - 1;\n    }\n  }\n}\n\ntemplate <typename KeyType>\nauto HyperLogLogPresto<KeyType>::AddElem(KeyType val) -> void {\n  if (num_buckets_ == 0) {\n    return;\n  }\n\n  hash_t hash = CalculateHash(val);\n\n  // Extract bucket index from the first n_leading_bits\n  uint16_t bucket_idx = hash & ((1UL << n_leading_bits_) - 1);\n\n  // Get the remaining bits by right-shifting\n  hash_t remaining = hash >> n_leading_bits_;\n\n  // Find the position of the leftmost 1 bit in remaining bits\n  uint8_t rho = 1;\n  if (remaining == 0) {\n    rho = 65;  // If all zeros, use a large value\n  } else {\n    // Count leading zeros + 1\n    while ((remaining & (1ULL << (63 - (rho - 1)))) == 0 && rho <= 64) {\n      rho++;\n    }\n  }\n\n  {\n    std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(mutex_);\n    UpdateBuckets(bucket_idx, rho);\n  }\n}\n\ntemplate <typename T>\nauto HyperLogLogPresto<T>::ComputeCardinality() -> void {\n  if (num_buckets_ == 0) {\n    cardinality_ = 0;\n    return;\n  }\n\n  std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(mutex_);\n\n  // Use the harmonic mean formula from HyperLogLog paper\n  double raw_estimate = 0.0;\n  for (size_t i = 0; i < num_buckets_; i++) {\n    uint64_t val = dense_bucket_[i].to_ullong();\n    // Check if there's an overflow value\n    if (overflow_bucket_.count(i) > 0) {\n      val = overflow_bucket_[i].to_ullong();\n    }\n    raw_estimate += std::pow(2.0, -static_cast<double>(val));\n  }\n\n  // HyperLogLog formula\n  double alpha = CONSTANT;\n  double m = static_cast<double>(num_buckets_);\n  cardinality_ = static_cast<uint64_t>(alpha * m * m / raw_estimate);\n}",

 // 2^n_bits\n    registers_.resize(num_buckets_, 0);\n  }\n}\n\ntemplate <typename KeyType>\nauto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::ComputeBinary(const hash_t &hash) const -> std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> {\n  std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> result;\n  for (int i = 0; i < BITSET_CAPACITY; i++) {\n    if ((hash >> i) & 1ULL) {\n      result[i] = 1;\n    }\n  }\n  return result;\n}\n\ntemplate <typename KeyType>\nauto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::PositionOfLeftmostOne(const std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> &bset) const -> uint64_t {\n  // Count leading zeros from the most significant bit and return position\n  // This is the position of the first 1 bit from the left, or BITSET_CAPACITY+1 if all zeros\n  for (int i = BITSET_CAPACITY - 1; i >= 0; i--) {\n    if (bset[i]) {\n      return BITSET_CAPACITY - i;  // Leading zeros + 1\n    }\n  }\n  return BITSET_CAPACITY + 1;  // All zeros\n}\n\ntemplate <typename KeyType>\nauto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::AddElem(KeyType val) -> void {\n  if (num_buckets_ == 0) {\n    return;\n  }\n\n  hash_t hash = CalculateHash(val);\n\n  // Extract bucket index from the first n_bits\n  size_t bucket_idx = hash & ((1UL << n_bits_) - 1);\n\n  // Get the remaining bits by right-shifting\n  hash_t remaining = hash >> n_bits_;\n\n  // Convert remaining bits to bitset and find position of leftmost 1\n  auto binary = ComputeBinary(remaining);\n  uint64_t rho = PositionOfLeftmostOne(binary);\n\n  // Update the register with maximum value\n  {\n    std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(mutex_);\n    if (rho > registers_[bucket_idx]) {\n      registers_[bucket_idx] = rho;\n    }\n  }\n}\n\ntemplate <typename KeyType>\nauto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::ComputeCardinality() -> void {\n  if (num_buckets_ == 0) {\n    cardinality_ = 0;\n    return;\n  }\n\n  std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(mutex_);\n\n  // Use the harmonic mean formula from HyperLogLog paper\n  double raw_estimate = 0.0;\n  for (size_t i = 0; i < num_buckets_; i++) {\n    raw_estimate += std::pow(2.0, -static_cast<double>(registers_[i]));\n  }\n\n  // HyperLogLog formula\n  double alpha = CONSTANT;\n  double m = static_cast<double>(num_buckets_);\n  cardinality_ = static_cast<size_t>(alpha * m * m / raw_estimate);\n}\n\ntemplate class HyperLogLog<int64_t>;\ntemplate class HyperLogLog<std::string>;\n\n}  // namespace bustub\n",

 // 2^n_leading_bits\n    dense_bucket_.resize(num_buckets_);\n  }\n}\n\ntemplate <typename KeyType>\nauto HyperLogLogPresto<KeyType>::UpdateBuckets(uint16_t bucket_idx, uint8_t rho) -> void {\n  // Get current value in dense bucket\n  auto &dense = dense_bucket_[bucket_idx];\n  uint64_t current_val = dense.to_ullong();\n\n  if (rho <= (1UL << DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE) - 1) {\n    // Value fits in dense bucket\n    if (rho > current_val) {\n      dense = rho;\n      // Clear overflow if it exists and we update dense\n      overflow_bucket_.erase(bucket_idx);\n    }\n  } else {\n    // Value needs to go to overflow bucket\n    auto &overflow = overflow_bucket_[bucket_idx];\n    uint64_t overflow_val = overflow.to_ullong();\n    // Store the overflow value\n    if (rho > overflow_val) {\n      overflow = rho;\n      // Also update dense to max value\n      dense = (1UL << DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE) - 1;\n    }\n  }\n}\n\ntemplate <typename KeyType>\nauto HyperLogLogPresto<KeyType>::AddElem(KeyType val) -> void {\n  if (num_buckets_ == 0) {\n    return;\n  }\n\n  hash_t hash = CalculateHash(val);\n\n  // Extract bucket index from the first n_leading_bits\n  uint16_t bucket_idx = hash & ((1UL << n_leading_bits_) - 1);\n\n  // Get the remaining bits by right-shifting\n  hash_t remaining = hash >> n_leading_bits_;\n\n  // Find the position of the leftmost 1 bit (count leading zeros + 1)\n  uint8_t rho;\n  if (remaining == 0) {\n    rho = 65; i < num_buckets_; i++) {\n    raw_estimate += std::pow(2.0, -static_cast<double>(registers_[i]));\n  }\n\n  // HyperLogLog formula\n  double alpha = CONSTANT;\n  double m = static_cast<double>(num_buckets_);\n  double estimate = alpha * m * m / raw_estimate;\n  // Round to nearest integer\n  cardinality_ = static_cast<size_t>(std::round(estimate));\n}\n\ntemplate class HyperLogLog<int64_t>;\ntemplate class HyperLogLog<std::string>;\n\n}  // namespace bustub\n",

 // 2^n_leading_bits\n    dense_bucket_.resize(num_buckets_);\n  }\n}\n\ntemplate <typename KeyType>\nauto HyperLogLogPresto<KeyType>::UpdateBuckets(uint16_t bucket_idx, uint8_t rho) -> void {\n  // Get current values\n  auto &dense = dense_bucket_[bucket_idx];\n  uint64_t current_dense = dense.to_ullong();\n\n  auto &overflow = overflow_bucket_[bucket_idx];\n  uint64_t current_overflow = overflow.to_ullong();\n\n  // Reconstruct the full rho value from dense + overflow\n  uint64_t current_full_rho = current_dense | (current_overflow << DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE);\n\n  if (rho > current_full_rho) {\n    // Update with the new value\n    dense = rho & ((1UL << DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE) - 1);   static inline auto HashBytes(const char *bytes, size_t length) -> hash_t {
    // https://github.com/greenplum-db/gpos/blob/b53c1acd6285de94044ff91fbee91589543feba1/libgpos/src/utils.cpp#L126
    hash_t hash = length;
    for (size_t i = 0; i < length; ++i) {

After
template <typename KeyType>
HyperLogLog<KeyType>::HyperLogLog(int16_t n_bits) : cardinality_(0), n_bits_(n_bits) {
  // Handle edge cases
  if (n_bits <= 0) {
    num_buckets_ = 0;
  } else {
    num_buckets_ = 1UL << n_bits;  // 2^n_bits
    registers_.resize(num_buckets_, 0);
  }
}

  std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> result;
  for (int i = 0; i < BITSET_CAPACITY; i++) {

After
template <typename KeyType>
auto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::PositionOfLeftmostOne(const std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> &bset) const -> uint64_t {
  // Find the position of the leftmost 1 bit (count leading zeros + 1)
  for (uint64_t i = 0; i < BITSET_CAPACITY; i++) {
    if (bset[i]) {
      return i + 1;  // Return position (1-indexed)
    }
  }
  return BITSET_CAPACITY + 1;  // All zeros
}
6. EDIT /workspace/bustub/src/primer/hyperloglog.cpp
Before
template <typename KeyType>
auto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::AddElem(KeyType val) -> void {
  /** @TODO(student) Implement this function! */
}
After
template <typename KeyType>
auto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::AddElem(KeyType val) -> void {
  if (num_buckets_ == 0) {
    return;
  }

  hash_t hash = CalculateHash(val);

  // Extract bucket index from the first n_bits
  size_t bucket_idx = hash & ((1UL << n_bits_) - 1);

  // Get the remaining bits by right-shifting
  hash_t remaining = hash >> n_bits_;

  // Convert remaining bits to bitset and find position of leftmost 1
  auto binary = ComputeBinary(remaining);
  uint64_t rho = PositionOfLeftmostOne(binary);

  // Update the register with maximum value
  {
    std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(mutex_);
    if (rho > registers_[bucket_idx]) {
      registers_[bucket_idx] = rho;
    }
  }
}
7. EDIT /workspace/bustub/src/primer/hyperloglog.cpp
Before
template <typename KeyType>
auto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::ComputeCardinality() -> void {
  /** @TODO(student) Implement this function! */
}
After
template <typename KeyType>
auto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::ComputeCardinality() -> void {
  if (num_buckets_ == 0) {
    cardinality_ = 0;
    return;
  }

  std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(mutex_);

  // Use the harmonic mean formula from HyperLogLog paper
  double raw_estimate = 0.0;
  for (size_t i = 0; i < num_buckets_; i++) {
    raw_estimate += std::pow(2.0, -static_cast<double>(registers_[i]));
  }

  // HyperLogLog formula
  double alpha = CONSTANT;
  double m = static_cast<double>(num_buckets_);
  cardinality_ = static_cast<size_t>(alpha * m * m / raw_estimate);
}

template <typename KeyType>

After
template <typename KeyType>
auto HyperLogLogPresto<KeyType>::UpdateBuckets(uint16_t bucket_idx, uint8_t rho) -> void {
  // Get current value in dense bucket
  auto &dense = dense_bucket_[bucket_idx];
  uint64_t current_val = dense.to_ullong();

  if (rho <= (1UL << DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE) - 1) {
    // Value fits in dense bucket
    if (rho > current_val) {
      dense = rho;
      // Clear overflow if it exists and we update dense
      overflow_bucket_.erase(bucket_idx);
    }
  } else {
    // Value needs to go to overflow bucket
    auto &overflow = overflow_bucket_[bucket_idx];
    uint64_t overflow_val = overflow.to_ullong();
    // Store the overflow value
    if (rho > overflow_val) {
      overflow = rho;
      // Also update dense to max value
      dense = (1UL << DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE) - 1;
    }
  }
}

template <typename KeyType>
auto HyperLogLogPresto<KeyType>::AddElem(KeyType val) -> void {
  if (num_buckets_ == 0) {
    return;
  }

  hash_t hash = CalculateHash(val);

  // Extract bucket index from the first n_leading_bits
  uint16_t bucket_idx = hash & ((1UL << n_leading_bits_) - 1);

  // Get the remaining bits by right-shifting
  hash_t remaining = hash >> n_leading_bits_;

  // Find the position of the leftmost 1 bit in remaining bits
  uint8_t rho = 1;
  if (remaining == 0) {
    rho = 65;  // If all zeros, use a large value
  } else {
    // Count leading zeros + 1
    while ((remaining & (1ULL << (63 - (rho - 1)))) == 0 && rho <= 64) {
      rho++;
    }
  }

  {
    std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(mutex_);
    UpdateBuckets(bucket_idx, rho);
  }
}

  if (num_buckets_ == 0) {
    cardinality_ = 0;
    return;
  }

  std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(mutex_);

  // Use the har

template <typename KeyType>
auto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::PositionOfLeftmostOne(const std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> &bset) const -> uint64_t {
  // Find the position of the leftmost 1 bit (count leading zeros + 1)
  for (uint64_t i = 0; i < BITSET_CAPACITY; i++) {
    if (bset[i]) {
      return i + 1;  // Return position (1-indexed)
    }
  }
  return BITSET_CAPACITY + 1;  // All zeros
}
After
template <typename KeyType>
auto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::ComputeBinary(const hash_t &hash) const -> std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> {
  std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> result;
  for (int i = 0; i < BITSET_CAPACITY; i++) {

template <typename KeyType>
auto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::PositionOfLeftmostOne(const std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> &bset) const -> uint64_t {
  // Count leading zeros from the most significant bit and return position
  // This is the position of the first 1 bit from the left, or BITSET_CAPACITY+1 if all zeros
  for (int i = BITSET_CAPACITY - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
    if (bset[i]) {
      return BITSET_CAPACITY - i;  // Leading zeros + 1
    }
  }
  return BITSET_CAPACITY + 1;  // All zeros
}

After
template <typename KeyType>
auto HyperLogLogPresto<KeyType>::AddElem(KeyType val) -> void {
  if (num_buckets_ == 0) {
    return;
  }

  hash_t hash = CalculateHash(val);

  // Extract bucket index from the first n_leading_bits
  uint16_t bucket_idx = hash & ((1UL << n_leading_bits_) - 1);

  // Get the remaining bits by right-shifting
  hash_t remaining = hash >> n_leading_bits_;

  // Find the position of the leftmost 1 bit (count leading zeros + 1)
  uint8_t rho;
  if (remaining == 0) {
    rho = 65;  // If all zeros, use a large value
  } else {
    // Count leading zeros by looking from MSB
    rho = 1;
    for (int i = 63; i >= 0; i--) {
      if ((remaining >> i) & 1ULL) {
        rho = 64 - i;  // Leading zeros + 1
        break;
      }
    }
  }

  {
    std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(mutex_);
    UpdateBuckets(bucket_idx, rho);
  }
}

After
template <typename KeyType>
auto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::AddElem(KeyType val) -> void {
  if (num_buckets_ == 0) {
    return;
  }

  hash_t hash = CalculateHash(val);

  // Extract bucket index from the highest n_bits
  size_t bucket_idx = hash >> (64 - n_bits_);
  if (n_bits_ == 0) {
    bucket_idx = 0;
  }

  // Get the remaining bits
  hash_t remaining = (hash << n_bits_) & ((n_bits_ == 0) ? hash : ((1UL << (64 - n_bits_)) - 1));
  if (n_bits_ == 0) {
    remaining = hash;
  }

  // Find position of the first 1 bit (count leading zeros + 1)
  uint64_t rho;
  if (remaining == 0) {
    rho = 65;
  } else {
    // Use __builtin_clzll to count leading zeros
    rho = __builtin_clzll(remaining) + 1;
  }

  // Update the register with maximum value
  {
    std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(mutex_);
    if (rho > registers_[bucket_idx]) {
      registers_[bucket_idx] = rho;
    }
  }
}

After
template <typename KeyType>
auto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::AddElem(KeyType val) -> void {
  if (num_buckets_ == 0) {
    return;
  }

  hash_t hash = CalculateHash(val);

  // Extract bucket index from the lowest n_bits
  size_t bucket_idx = hash & ((1UL << n_bits_) - 1);

  // Get the remaining bits by right-shifting
  hash_t remaining = hash >> n_bits_;

  // Find position of the first 1 bit (count leading zeros in remaining bits + 1)
  uint64_t rho;
  if (remaining == 0) {
    rho = 65;
  } else {
    // Count leading zeros in the remaining (64-n_bits_) bits
    // __builtin_clzll counts leading zeros in a 64-bit value
    // We need to shift left to align to the MSB
    uint64_t shifted = remaining << n_bits_;
    rho = __builtin_clzll(shifted) + 1;
  }

  // Update the register with maximum value
  {
    std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(mutex_);
    if (rho > registers_[bucket_idx]) {
      registers_[bucket_idx] = rho;
    }
  }
}

    // Use __builtin_ctzll to count trailing zeros (from the right)
    rho = __builtin_ctzll(remaining) + 1;
  }

32. EDIT /workspace/bustub/src/primer/hyperloglog_presto.cpp
Before
template <typename KeyType>
auto HyperLogLogPresto<KeyType>::UpdateBuckets(uint16_t bucket_idx, uint8_t rho) -> void {
  // Get current value in dense bucket
  auto &dense = dense_bucket_[bucket_idx];
  uint64_t current_val = dense.to_ullong();

  if (rho <= (1UL << DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE) - 1) {
    // Value fits in dense bucket
    if (rho > current_val) {
      dense = rho;
      // Clear overflow if it exists and we update dense
      overflow_bucket_.erase(bucket_idx);
    }
  } else {
    // Value needs to go to overflow bucket
    auto &overflow = overflow_bucket_[bucket_idx];
    uint64_t overflow_val = overflow.to_ullong();
    // Store the overflow value
    if (rho > overflow_val) {
      overflow = rho;
      // Also update dense to max value
      dense = (1UL << DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE) - 1;
    }
  }
}
After
template <typename KeyType>
auto HyperLogLogPresto<KeyType>::UpdateBuckets(uint16_t bucket_idx, uint8_t rho) -> void {
  // Get current values
  auto &dense = dense_bucket_[bucket_idx];
  uint64_t current_dense = dense.to_ullong();

  auto &overflow = overflow_bucket_[bucket_idx];
  uint64_t current_overflow = overflow.to_ullong();

  // Reconstruct the full rho value from dense + overflow
  uint64_t current_full_rho = current_dense | (current_overflow << DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE);

  if (rho > current_full_rho) {
    // Update with the new value
    dense = rho & ((1UL << DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE) - 1);  // Lower 4 bits
    if (rho > (1UL << DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE) - 1) {
      // Need to store overflow
      overflow = rho >> DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE;  // Upper bits
    } else {
      // Clear overflow
      overflow_bucket_.erase(bucket_idx);
    }
  }
}

Before
  // Use the harmonic mean formula from HyperLogLog paper
  double raw_estimate = 0.0;
  for (size_t i = 0; i < num_buckets_; i++) {
    uint64_t val = dense_bucket_[i].to_ullong();
    // Check if there's an overflow value
    if (overflow_bucket_.count(i) > 0) {
      val = overflow_bucket_[i].to_ullong();
    }
    raw_estimate += std::pow(2.0, -static_cast<double>(val));
  }
After
  // Use the harmonic mean formula from HyperLogLog paper
  double raw_estimate = 0.0;
  for (size_t i = 0; i < num_buckets_; i++) {
    uint64_t dense_val = dense_bucket_[i].to_ullong();
    uint64_t full_rho = dense_val;

    // Reconstruct full rho from dense + overflow if overflow exists
    if (overflow_bucket_.count(i) > 0) {
      uint64_t overflow_val = overflow_bucket_[i].to_ullong();
      full_rho = dense_val | (overflow_val << DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE);
    }

    raw_estimate += std::pow(2.0, -static_cast<double>(full_rho));
  }
36. EDIT /workspace/bustub/src/primer/hyperloglog_presto.cpp
Before
template <typename KeyType>
auto HyperLogLogPresto<KeyType>::UpdateBuckets(uint16_t bucket_idx, uint8_t rho) -> void {
  // Get current values
  auto &dense = dense_bucket_[bucket_idx];
  uint64_t current_dense = dense.to_ullong();

  auto &overflow = overflow_bucket_[bucket_idx];
  uint64_t current_overflow = overflow.to_ullong();

  // Reconstruct the full rho value from dense + overflow
  uint64_t current_full_rho = current_dense | (current_overflow << DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE);

  if (rho > current_full_rho) {
    // Update with the new value
    dense = rho & ((1UL << DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE) - 1);  // Lower 4 bits
    if (rho > (1UL << DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE) - 1) {
      // Need to store overflow
      overflow = rho >> DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE;  // Upper bits
    } else {
      // Clear overflow
      overflow_bucket_.erase(bucket_idx);
    }
  }
}
After
template <typename KeyType>
auto HyperLogLogPresto<KeyType>::UpdateBuckets(uint16_t bucket_idx, uint8_t rho) -> void {
  // Get current values
  uint64_t current_dense = dense_bucket_[bucket_idx].to_ullong();
  uint64_t current_overflow = 0;

  if (overflow_bucket_.count(bucket_idx) > 0) {
    current_overflow = overflow_bucket_[bucket_idx].to_ullong();
  }

  // Reconstruct the full rho value from dense + overflow
  uint64_t current_full_rho = current_dense | (current_overflow << DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE);

  if (rho > current_full_rho) {
    // Update with the new value
    dense_bucket_[bucket_idx] = rho & ((1UL << DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE) - 1);  // Lower 4 bits
    if (rho > (1UL << DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE) - 1) {
      // Need to store overflow
      overflow_bucket_[bucket_idx] = rho >> DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE;  // Upper bits
    } else {
      // Clear overflow
      overflow_bucket_.erase(bucket_idx);
    }
  }
}
